RACE OVERVIEW
=============
The 2024 Las Vegas Grand Prix saw George Russell of Mercedes take the win, followed by his teammate Lewis Hamilton, securing a one-two finish for the team. Carlos Sainz Jr. of Ferrari completed the podium in third place. Max Verstappen of Red Bull Racing finished fifth, a result that clinched his fourth consecutive World Drivers' Championship. The race, held on the Las Vegas Strip Circuit, had some exciting moments, including Charles Leclerc initially gaining positions at the start and later dueling with Verstappen. Several drivers, including Pierre Gasly and Alexander Albon, had to retire due to mechanical issues.
